## ğŸ¤” What is Christmas Cards Maker?

**Christmas Cards Maker** is a creative tool powered by Google's Nano Banana Pro for generating beautiful Christmas cards:

- ğŸ¯ **AI-Powered Generation** - Create stunning cards with simple prompts
- ğŸ¨ **Diverse Styles** - From traditional to modern, cartoon to realistic
- âš¡ **Personalized Messages** - Add your own greetings and wishes
- ğŸŒˆ **High-Quality Output** - Print-ready resolution
- ğŸ”§ **Fast Creation** - Generate cards in seconds
- ğŸ“ **Multiple Themes** - Santa, snowflakes, trees, and more

ğŸ“š learnMore

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

### No. 1: Sloth Hanging from Candy Cane Christmas Card

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An adorable printable Christmas card design featuring a slow-moving sloth hanging from a candy cane, trying to reach a Christmas tree. This prompt is perfect for creating charming and funny holiday greetings with a unique touch.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
An adorable printable Christmas card design, aspect ratio 1:1.4. A cute, slow-moving sloth hangs upside down from a candy cane that stretches horizontally across the top of the card. The sloth is wearing a festive ugly Christmas sweater with a pixelated snowflake pattern. He is holding a star tree topper in his slow claws, trying to reach a Christmas tree that is just out of frame. The background is a solid deep teal color to make the sloth pop. Below the sloth, the text reads: {argument name="text" default="Slowly getting into the Spirit"} in a relaxed, hand-lettered font.
```

### No. 2: Polar Bear and Penguin Scarf Christmas Card

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A heartwarming and whimsical Christmas card cover depicting an unlikely friendship between a massive polar bear and a tiny penguin, connected by a comically oversized scarf. Ideal for conveying themes of friendship and warmth during the holidays.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A heartwarming and whimsical Christmas card cover, aspect ratio 1:1.4. A massive, fluffy white polar bear sits on the left, and a tiny, round penguin stands on the right against a clean, ice-blue background. They are connected by a comically long, oversized red and green knitted scarf that is wrapped multiple times around the bear's neck and then loops down to wrap snugly around the tiny penguin. The penguin is looking up at the bear with admiration. The texture of the fur and the knit wool is visible and soft. Simple white snowflakes fall gently around them. No text, just a sweet image of friendship.
```

### No. 3: Gingerbread Yoga Class Christmas Card

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A cheerful and adorable printable Christmas card design featuring five cute gingerbread men cookies in a 'Yoga Class'. This prompt is perfect for creating heartwarming holiday greetings with a touch of humor and cuteness.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A funny and adorable printable Christmas card design, aspect ratio 1:1.4. The background is a solid, clean pastel mint green. The illustration features a "Yoga Class" of five cute gingerbread men cookies. The central gingerbread man is standing on one leg in a "Tree Pose," balancing a gumdrop on his head with a focused expression. To his left, another cookie is attempting a "Downward Dog" pose but his arm has crumbled slightly, revealing delicious cookie crumbs. To the right, a gingerbread man is meditating in "Lotus position" with his icing eyes closed. They all have white icing details and red red-hot candy buttons. The style is a clean, flat vector illustration with soft shadows. Text at the top reads: {argument name="text" default="Find Your Inner Piece"} in a playful, rounded white font.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt creates a cozy, tactile Christmas card design that looks like handmade felt appliquÃ© stitching, featuring a cute fox cub in a snowy scene. Perfect for unique and crafty holiday visuals.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A cozy, tactile Christmas card design, aspect ratio 1:1.4. The illustration looks entirely like handmade felt appliquÃ© stitching. A cute orange fox cub made of fuzzy felt fabric sits in layers of white felt snow, looking up at a felt Christmas tree decorated with colorful button ornaments. The texture of the wool fibers and the stitching around the edges is clearly visible. The background is a soft blue felt sky.
```

### No. 5: Pug with Reindeer Antlers and Clown Nose

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt generates a funny and cute printable card featuring a close-up photographic portrait of a pug reluctantly wearing reindeer antlers and a glowing red clown nose. Ideal for humorous and quirky holiday greetings.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A funny and cute printable card, aspect ratio 1:1.4. A close-up photographic portrait of a chubby pug dog's face. It is reluctantly wearing a headband with brown felt reindeer antlers and a very bright, glowing red clown nose over its own nose. The pug has a serious, slightly judging expression, staring straight at the camera. The background is blurred festive red lights.
```

### No. 6: Alpaca Overloaded with Presents

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/â­-Featured-gold)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt creates a cute and chaotic Christmas card featuring a fluffy alpaca overloaded with a precarious stack of Christmas presents. Perfect for humorous and charming holiday greetings.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A cute and chaotic Christmas card, aspect ratio 1:1.4. A fluffy white alpaca stands against a solid mint green background. Its back is overloaded with an impossibly tall, precarious stack of colorful wrapped Christmas presents with bows that are wobbling wildly. The alpaca has a patient, slightly strained expression, and its skinny legs are shaking slightly under the weight.
```

### No. 2: Christmas Koalas Â· Can't-Let-Go Frame

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This prompt creates an animated Christmas photo frame in a vertical 1:1.4 format. The border features cartoon koalas hugging ornaments and garlands, refusing to let go, creating gentle, cozy humor in a print-ready design.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A printable animated Christmas photo frame in vertical 1:1.4 format.

Frame-only design.

A blank photo placeholder is centered both horizontally and vertically, 1:1.4 aspect ratio, 70% width, completely untouched.
```

### No. 68: Folk Art Stockings for Special Relative

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed flat design featuring patterned folk art stockings with gold accents. This card is perfect for personalized greetings, with customizable fields for recipient names (e.g., "Niece").

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A high-quality, printable Christmas greeting card illustration in a charming, whimsical flat design, aspect ratio 1:1.4.

The scene features three decorative Christmas stockings hanging in a slight diagonal line from the top against a clean off-white background. Each stocking is uniquely decorated with folk art and retro-inspired patterns, using a festive color palette of red, dark green, pink, teal, blue, and gold. The stockings have prominent gold glitter accents along their edges and on some patterns, giving them a sparkling, textured feel.

Small, stylized robins with red breasts are perched on the cuffs of the stockings, which are filled with small, wrapped gift boxes. Hanging from the top are decorative elements like strings of colorful beads, diamond-shaped garlands, and a single pink retro bauble.

The background is sprinkled with gold foil dots and starbursts, creating a magical, confetti-like atmosphere.

At the bottom of the card, the text is displayed. The phrase "{argument name="greeting line 1" default="To a"}" is in a delicate black script. Below it, the main greeting "{argument name="greeting line 2" default="WONDERFUL NIECE"}" is in a large, stylized, uppercase font. The word "WONDERFUL" is rendered in a gold foil effect, while the word "NIECE" has each letter filled with a different solid color from the card's palette.
```

```
At the top, the greeting {argument name="text" default="Merry Christmas"} is written in a decorative, vintage font, appearing as if formed from snow on a dark eave.
```

```
The background is a solid, rich burgundy red. A prominent golden arch frames the upper half of the card, decorated with small, scattered golden stars and sparkles. At the apex of the arch is a larger, radiant golden star.

Below the hanging ornaments, the greeting {argument name="Greeting" default="Merry Christmas"} is written in an elegant, flowing golden script.

The entire design is enclosed by a sophisticated double golden line border. The inner border features a repeating pattern of 'x's and dots, with a simple heart outline centered at the bottom. Two golden bells with radiating lines are placed in the top corners of the card. The overall aesthetic is clean, festive, and sophisticated with a metallic gold finish on all line work and text.
```

A classic, detailed painting of a jolly Santa Claus reading a scroll in a snowy forest. He is surrounded by a decorated tree and curious woodland animals under a lantern's glow.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
An exquisite, highly detailed printable Christmas illustration in a classic painterly style. A jolly Santa Claus, dressed in his traditional red suit with white fur trim, stands in a snowy forest clearing at night, smiling as he reads from a long parchment scroll.

To his left is a beautifully decorated Christmas tree, its branches laden with snow, colorful baubles, and lights, topped with a glowing star that illuminates the scene. Several wrapped presents in red, blue, and gold paper are nestled at the base of the tree. Behind Santa, his large green toy sack rests in the snow.

In the foreground, a vintage lantern casts a warm, golden glow on the snow, where a charming group of woodland creatures have gathered. Two curious squirrels, two fluffy rabbits, and several small birds watch Santa with wonder.

Gentle snowflakes fall through the air, blanketing the entire scene. In the distant background, a quaint village with a church steeple is visible among the snow-covered pine trees, all under a deep blue winter night sky. The artwork has a magical, heartwarming atmosphere, with a beautiful interplay of warm and cool light and rich textures.

--ar 1:1.4
```

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
An exquisite and elegant printable Christmas card design, front view, flat lay. The design is on a clean, minimalist white card background.

This layered composition features three prominent poinsettias made of sparkling red glitter paper with tiny gold centers, layered over a mix of dark green paper leaves, shiny gold foil leaves, and delicate white paper sprigs. A simple loop of cream-colored grosgrain ribbon is attached to the top of the gold ring.

Inside the right side of the ring, the text {argument name="text" default="Merry Christmas"} is written in elegant gold foil. The word 'Merry' is in a clean uppercase font, and 'Christmas' is in a flowing script.

The overall style is sophisticated, high-end, and celebrates texture with glitter, foil, and layered paper. High resolution, printable quality, 1:1.4 aspect ratio.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A beautiful, high-quality, printable Christmas greeting card, presented in a flat lay, top-down view. The card showcases an intricate and elegant paper quilling design. The centerpiece features two large, vibrant golden-yellow Christmas bells, meticulously crafted from quilled paper strips, with rich brown rims and delicate coiled clappers.

Tied at the top of the bells is a large, luxurious bow made from deep red paper, its edges sparkling with fine gold glitter. Spilling out from behind the bow are festive arrangements of deep green holly leaves with defined outlines and clusters of bright red berries, all created with the same detailed paper quilling technique, giving the art a subtle 3D relief effect.

The entire artwork is mounted on a clean, textured white cardstock background, framed by a simple, crisp red border. The scene is illuminated with bright, even, and soft lighting. In the top right corner, display the text: {argument name="Text" default="Christmas Bells"}.

The overall aesthetic is handmade, festive, and exceptionally detailed. Aspect ratio 1:1.4.
```

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
An exquisite, printable Christmas greeting card illustration of a peaceful woodland scene at night, in a classic, detailed painterly style.

The scene features a snow-covered landscape under a deep blue starry sky, with a large, brilliant eight-pointed star, the Star of Bethlehem, shining brightly in the upper left. A central, snow-laden evergreen tree is adorned with a variety of friendly animals.

A gentle, spotted fawn stands on the left. Gathered at the base of the tree are a fluffy brown rabbit, a curious raccoon, and two red cardinals on the snowy ground. Perched in the tree are a white dove at the very top, another red cardinal, a black-capped chickadee, and a vibrant bluebird on the lower branches. A second chickadee is captured in mid-flight, approaching the tree.

The background shows a distant forest of snow-dusted pines. The lighting is soft and magical, casting gentle blue shadows on the pristine snow. The overall mood is serene, harmonious, and heartwarming.
```

### No. 120: Minimalist Hanging Ornaments Graphic

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A clean, modern flat graphic design featuring five distinct Christmas ornaments hanging from strings against a solid white background, with customizable elegant script text below.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
An exquisite, printable Christmas card design with a modern, minimalist flat graphic style, aspect ratio 1:1.4.
The design is set against a clean, solid white background.

Across the top, five Christmas ornaments hang from thin black strings at varying heights.
From left to right, the ornaments are: a large green bauble with sparkling silver glitter snowflakes; a small, plain red bauble; a small bauble completely covered in shimmering silver glitter; a large red bauble featuring a central white snowflake cutout; and a medium-sized, plain green bauble.

Centered below the ornaments, the text {argument name="Greeting" default="Merry Christmas"} is elegantly written in a flowing, black script font.
```

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-christmas-card-prompts/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
